# Text Elements
Energy is used to weaken bonds
and convert into a gas ^wYfE7kGz

Q. How much energy does one need
to release so that steam -> Water of 20g
Given that it is at 100C
-> Specific Later H.V = 340 J/g ^rpdG4FfJ

Q. How much energy does one need
to boil water of 20g
Given that it is at 100C
-> Specific Latent H.V = 340 J/g ^zEPnor7E
